SET LINESIZE 200
SET PAGESIZE 200

DROP TABLE delivery_address;
DROP TABLE vip_subscription;
DROP TABLE orders_items;
DROP TABLE rating_items;
DROP TABLE orders;
DROP TABLE payment;
DROP TABLE delivery;
DROP TABLE delivery_company;
DROP TABLE pickup;
DROP TABLE promotion;
DROP TABLE voucher;
DROP TABLE rating_delivery;
DROP TABLE rating_restaurant;
DROP TABLE items;
DROP TABLE restaurant;
DROP TABLE rating_restaurant;
DROP TABLE member;


--Member table
CREATE TABLE member (
	member_id 		VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	member_name 		VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
	member_email 		VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
	phone 			VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
	member_type 		VARCHAR2(20) DEFAULT 'NORMAL' NOT NULL,
	registration_date 		DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NOT NULL,
	PRIMARY KEY (member_id),
CONSTRAINT uq_member_email UNIQUE (member_email),
	CONSTRAINT chk_member_type CHECK (member_type IN ('NORMAL', 'VIP'))
);




--Restaurant table
CREATE TABLE restaurant (
  	restaurant_id 		VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
 	 restaurant_name 		VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
 	 restaurant_category 	VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
 	 restaurant_location 	VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
  	restaurant_phone 		VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
  	restaurant_avg_rating 	NUMBER(5,2) NOT NULL,
 	 PRIMARY KEY (restaurant_id),
  	CONSTRAINT chk_restaurant_category CHECK (restaurant_category IN ('HALAL', 'NON-HALAL')),
 	 CONSTRAINT chk_restaurant_avg_rating CHECK (restaurant_avg_rating BETWEEN 0 AND 5)
);



--Items table
CREATE TABLE items (
	items_id 		VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	items_name 	VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
	items_price 	NUMBER(8,2) NOT NULL,
	items_type 	VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
	promotion 	VARCHAR2(100) DEFAULT 'NO' NOT NULL,
	restaurant_id 	VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (items_id),
	FOREIGN KEY (restaurant_id) REFERENCES restaurant(restaurant_id),
	CONSTRAINT chk_item_id_format CHECK (items_id LIKE 'R%F%'),
	CONSTRAINT chk_price CHECK (items_price > 0),
	CONSTRAINT chk_items_type CHECK (items_type IN ('FOOD', 'BEVERAGE', 'DESSERT')),
CONSTRAINT chk_promotion CHECK (promotion IN ('YES', 'NO'))
);


--Rating_restaurant table
CREATE TABLE rating_restaurant(
	rating_restaurant_id 	VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	restaurant_score  		NUMBER(1) NOT NULL,
	rating_date 		DATE NOT NULL,
	rating_comment 		VARCHAR2(300) NOT NULL,
	restaurant_id  		VARCHAR2(10),
	PRIMARY KEY (rating_restaurant_id),
FOREIGN KEY (restaurant_id) REFERENCES restaurant(restaurant_id),
	CONSTRAINT chk_restaurant_score CHECK (restaurant_score  BETWEEN 1 AND 5)
);




--Rating_delivery table
CREATE TABLE rating_delivery(
	rating_delivery_id 	VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	delivery_score 	NUMBER(1) NOT NULL,
	rating_date 	DATE NOT NULL,
	rating_comment 	VARCHAR2(300) NOT NULL,
	PRIMARY KEY (rating_delivery_id),
	CONSTRAINT chk_delivery_score CHECK (delivery_score  BETWEEN 1 AND 5)
);



--Voucher table
CREATE TABLE voucher(
	voucher_id 	VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	voucher_code 	NUMBER(1) NOT NULL,
	expiry_date DATE NOT NULL,
	description VARCHAR2(300) NOT NULL ,
	PRIMARY KEY (voucher_id)
);


--Promotion table
CREATE TABLE promotion(
	promotion_id 		VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	promo_name 		VARCHAR2(100)  NOT NULL,
	promo_description	                VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
	start_date	                                DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NOT NULL,
	end_date	                                DATE NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (promotion_id),
CONSTRAINT chk_promo_dates CHECK (end_date >= start_date)
);



--Pickup table
CREATE TABLE pickup(
	pickup_id 	VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	pickup_date            	DATE NOT NULL,
	pickup_status 	VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
pickup_person        	VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
	pickup_contact 	VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
	PRIMARY KEY (pickup_id),
	CONSTRAINT chk_pickup_status CHECK (pickup_status IN ('PENDING', 'PICKUP', 'CANCELLED'))
);


--Delivery_company table
CREATE TABLE delivery_company(
	delivery_company_id 	VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	delivery_name 		VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
	delivery_phone                       VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
	PRIMARY KEY (delivery_company_id)
);



--Delivery table
CREATE TABLE delivery(
	delivery_id 		VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	driver_name 		VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
	driver_phone                          VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
	car_plate_no 		VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
	delivery_company_id 	VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	rating_delivery_id 		VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	PRIMARY KEY (delivery_id),
	FOREIGN KEY (delivery_company_id) REFERENCES delivery_company(delivery_company_id),
	FOREIGN KEY (rating_delivery_id ) REFERENCES rating_delivery(rating_delivery_id )
);



--Payment  table
CREATE TABLE payment(
	payment_id 		VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	payment_method 		VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
	payment_amount 		NUMBER(8,2) NOT NULL,
payment_date                         DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NOT NULL,
	payment_status                      VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	PRIMARY KEY (payment_id),
CONSTRAINT chk_payment_method CHECK (payment_method IN ('Online Banking', 'TNG', 'Card Payment')),
	CONSTRAINT chk_payment_amount CHECK (payment_amount > 0),
CONSTRAINT chk_payment_status CHECK (payment_status IN ('PENDING', 'SUCCESS', 'FAILURE'))
);



--Orders table
CREATE TABLE orders(
	orders_id 		VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	orders_date 		DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NOT NULL,
	orders_amount 		NUMBER(8,2) NOT NULL,
	orders_type 		VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
	orders_status  		VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
	delivery_fee   		NUMBER(8,2) DEFAULT 0,
	delivery_date 		DATE,
	discount_name  		VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
discount_rate                      	NUMBER(5,2) NOT NULL,
payment_id                             VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
member_id 		VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
delivery_id 		VARCHAR2(10),
pickup_id 		VARCHAR2(10),
voucher_id 		VARCHAR2(10), 
PRIMARY KEY (orders_id),
FOREIGN KEY (payment_id) REFERENCES payment(payment_id),
	FOREIGN KEY (member_id) REFERENCES member(member_id),
	FOREIGN KEY (delivery_id ) REFERENCES delivery(delivery_id),
	FOREIGN KEY (pickup_id) REFERENCES pickup(pickup_id),
FOREIGN KEY (voucher_id ) REFERENCES voucher(voucher_id),
CONSTRAINT chk_orders_amount CHECK (orders_amount > 0),
	CONSTRAINT chk_orders_type CHECK (orders_type IN ('DELIVERY', 'PICKUP')),
	CONSTRAINT chk_order_type_logic CHECK ((orders_type = 'DELIVERY' AND delivery_id IS NOT NULL AND pickup_id IS NULL AND delivery_fee > 0) OR (orders_type = 'PICKUP' AND pickup_id IS NOT NULL AND delivery_id IS NULL AND delivery_fee = 0)),
CONSTRAINT chk_orders_status CHECK (orders_status IN ('PENDING', 'SUCCESS', 'FAILURE'))
);



--Rating_items table
CREATE TABLE rating_items(
	rating_item_id                      VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	item_score                            NUMBER(1) NOT NULL,
	rating_date                          DATE  NOT NULL,
	rating_comment                 VARCHAR2(300),
	PRIMARY KEY (rating_item_id),
	CONSTRAINT chk_item_score CHECK (item_score  BETWEEN 1 AND 5)
);



--Orders_items table
CREATE TABLE orders_items(
	orders_id  	VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
items_id 	 	VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	quantity 	         	NUMBER(8,2) NOT NULL,
	unit_price  	 NUMBER(8,2) NOT NULL,
	subtotal	 	NUMBER(8,2) NOT NULL,
	rating_item_id  	VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	PRIMARY KEY (orders_id, items_id),
	FOREIGN KEY (items_id) REFERENCES items(items_id),
	FOREIGN KEY (orders_id) REFERENCES orders(orders_id),
FOREIGN KEY (rating_item_id) REFERENCES rating_items(rating_item_id),
	CONSTRAINT chk_unit_price CHECK (unit_price > 0),
	CONSTRAINT chk_quantity CHECK (quantity > 0),
CONSTRAINT subtotal CHECK (subtotal > 0)
);	



--Vip_subscription table
CREATE TABLE vip_subscription(
	member_id  	VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	payment_id  	VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	amount	 	NUMBER(8,2) NOT NULL,
	payment_date  	DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NOT NULL,
	start_date	  	DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NOT NULL,
	end_date  	DATE NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (member_id, payment_id),
	FOREIGN KEY (member_id) REFERENCES member(member_id),
	FOREIGN KEY (payment_id) REFERENCES payment (payment_id),
	CONSTRAINT chk_vip_sub_amount CHECK (amount > 0),
CONSTRAINT chk_vip_date_range CHECK (end_date > start_date)
);


--Delivery_address table
CREATE TABLE delivery_address (
	delivery_address_id  	VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	member_id	               	VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
	address	                               	VARCHAR2(200) NOT NULL,
	contact_number 	 	VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
	contact_person	              	 VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
	PRIMARY KEY (delivery_address_id, member_id),
	FOREIGN KEY(member_id) REFERENCES member (member_id)
);

COLUMN table_name FORMAT A20
COLUMN total_records FORMAT 999999

--Show table name and total Record 
COLUMN table_name FORMAT A20
COLUMN total_records FORMAT 999999
SET SQLBLANKLINES ON

WITH record_counts AS (
    SELECT 'member' AS table_name, COUNT(*) AS total_records FROM member
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 'restaurant', COUNT(*) FROM restaurant
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 'rating_restaurant', COUNT(*) FROM rating_restaurant
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 'delivery_company', COUNT(*) FROM delivery_company
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 'voucher', COUNT(*) FROM voucher
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 'promotion', COUNT(*) FROM promotion
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 'rating_delivery', COUNT(*) FROM rating_delivery
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 'rating_items', COUNT(*) FROM rating_items
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 'pickup', COUNT(*) FROM pickup
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 'payment', COUNT(*) FROM payment
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 'items', COUNT(*) FROM items
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 'delivery', COUNT(*) FROM delivery
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 'delivery_address', COUNT(*) FROM delivery_address
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 'orders', COUNT(*) FROM orders
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 'orders_items', COUNT(*) FROM orders_items
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 'vip_subscription', COUNT(*) FROM vip_subscription
)
SELECT table_name, total_records FROM record_counts
UNION ALL
SELECT '--------------------', NULL FROM dual
UNION ALL
SELECT 'GRAND TOTAL', SUM(total_records) FROM record_counts;


--UPDATE NOT LOGIC RECORD

--update orders record

UPDATE orders o
SET o.orders_amount = (
    SELECT SUM(oi.subtotal)
    FROM orders_items oi
    WHERE oi.orders_id = o.orders_id
) + NVL(o.delivery_fee, 0) - NVL(o.discount_rate, 0)
WHERE o.orders_id BETWEEN 'O001' AND 'O120';

--update payment record

UPDATE payment p
SET p.payment_amount = (
    SELECT o.orders_amount 
    FROM orders o 
    WHERE o.payment_id = p.payment_id
)
WHERE EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 
    FROM orders o 
    WHERE o.payment_id = p.payment_id
);

UPDATE payment p
SET p.payment_amount = 6.00
WHERE p.payment_id NOT IN (SELECT payment_id FROM orders WHERE payment_id IS NOT NULL);
